ENTRY       EC 1.5.1.3                  Enzyme
NAME        dihydrofolate reductase;
            tetrahydrofolate dehydrogenase;
            DHFR;
            pteridine reductase:dihydrofolate reductase;
            dihydrofolate reductase:thymidylate synthase;
            thymidylate synthetase-dihydrofolate reductase;
            folic acid reductase;
            folic reductase;
            dihydrofolic acid reductase;
            dihydrofolic reductase;
            7,8-dihydrofolate reductase;
            NADPH-dihydrofolate reductase
CLASS       Oxidoreductases;
            Acting on the CH-NH group of donors;
            With NAD+ or NADP+ as acceptor
SYSNAME     5,6,7,8-tetrahydrofolate:NADP+ oxidoreductase
REACTION    5,6,7,8-tetrahydrofolate + NADP+ = 7,8-dihydrofolate + NADPH + H+ [RN:R00939]
ALL_REAC    R00939;
            (other) R00936 R00937 R00940 R02235 R02236 R11765
SUBSTRATE   5,6,7,8-tetrahydrofolate [CPD:C00101];
            NADP+ [CPD:C00006]
PRODUCT     7,8-dihydrofolate [CPD:C00415];
            NADPH [CPD:C00005];
            H+ [CPD:C00080]
COMMENT     The enzyme from animals and some micro-organisms also slowly reduces folate to 5,6,7,8-tetrahydrofolate.
HISTORY     EC 1.5.1.3 created 1961, modified 1976 (EC 1.5.1.4 created 1961, incorporated 1976)
